<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высота́</a> (1191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vysotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высоты́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>height (distance from bottom to top)</li>
<li>altitude, elevation</li>
<li>height <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an area of high altitude</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hill</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высотный.html>высо́тный</a> (13274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высота.html>высота́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сохнуть.html>со́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sóxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высохнуть.html>вы́сохнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsoxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высыхать.html>высыха́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сохнуть.html>со́хнуть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:высохший.html>вы́сохший</a> (10448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высохший.html>вы́сохший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výsoxšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высохнуть.html>вы́сохнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsoxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***выставить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выставить.html>вы́ставить</a> (2686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выставить.html>вы́ставить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstavitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выставлять.html>выставля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put forward, to move out, to put outside, to bring forward, to place in front</li>
<li>to set out, to display, to present</li>
<li>to flaunt</li>
<li>to propose, to suggest</li>
<li>to put down (marks), to mark (as in school)</li>
<li>to expose</li></ol>

***выставлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выставлять.html>выставля́ть</a> (8067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выставить.html>вы́ставить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výstavitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выставлять.html>выставля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vystavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выставить.html>вы́ставить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put forward, to move out, to put outside, to bring forward, to place in front</li>
<li>to set out, to display, to present</li>
<li>to flaunt</li>
<li>to propose, to suggest</li>
<li>to put down (marks), to mark (as in school)</li>
<li>to expose</li></ol>

***выстоять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстоять.html>вы́стоять</a> (12684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстоять.html>вы́стоять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstojatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выста́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand (for a long time), to remain standing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выстоять.html>вы́стояли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́тами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:концерт.html>конце́рт</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sevódnja my <b>výstojali</b> dva časá za bilétami na koncért.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Today we stood for two hours (to buy) tickets for the concert.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to withstand, to bear (difficulty), to resist (an enemy), to survive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выстоять.html>вы́стояли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:война.html>войне́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní <b>výstojali</b> i pobedíli v étoj vojné.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They survived and won in this war.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***выстрадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстрадать.html>вы́страдать</a> (23975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страдать.html>страда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stradátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстрадать.html>вы́страдать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výstradatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to suffer, to endure</li>
<li>to gain/achieve through much suffering</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страдать.html>страда́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stradátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пострадать.html>пострада́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postradátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страдание.html>страда́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stradánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страда.html>страда́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stradá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выстраивать.html>выстра́ивать</a> (19498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстроить.html>вы́строить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výstroitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстраивать.html>выстра́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vystráivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстроить.html>вы́строить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to build</li>
<li>to line up, to draw up, to form up</li>
<li>to arrange</li>
<li><i>(a structure, a theory)</i> to build, to develop</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстраивать.html>выстра́ивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vystráivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстраиваться.html>выстра́иваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vystráivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстроиться.html>вы́строиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw up, to form, to line up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выстраиваться.html>выстра́иваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́чередь</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vystráivatʹsja</b> v óčeredʹ (za)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to queue up (for), to line up (for)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выстраивать.html>выстра́ивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vystráivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
